#Setup SOJ
sov_spawn_soj_scw = {
    every_state = {
        limit = {
            is_core_of = SOV
            is_owned_by = SOV
            NOT = {
                state = 408
                state = 409
                state = 560
                state = 655
                state = 537
                state = 657
                state = 561
                state = 574
                state = 562
                state = 637
                state = 644
                state = 563

                state = 569

                state = 571

                state = 822
                state = 824
                state = 882
                state = 878
                state = 876
                state = 877
                state = 874
                state = 875
            }
        }
        SOJ = {
            add_state_core = PREV
            transfer_state = PREV
        }
    }
    every_state = {
        limit = {
            is_core_of = UKR
            is_owned_by = UKR
        }
        SOJ = {
            add_state_core = PREV
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = control_caucasus
            }
        }
        every_state = {
            limit = {
                is_owned_by = SOJ
                OR = {
                    state = 233
                    state = 232
                    state = 235
                    state = 234
                    state = 827
                    state = 828
                    state = 821
                }
            }
            SOV = {
                transfer_state = PREV
            }
        }
    }
    SOV = {
        every_character = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    is_character = SOV_Georgy_zhukov
                    is_character = SOV_Aleksandr_vasilevsky
                    is_character = SOV_Boris_shaposhnikov
                    is_character = SOV_Nikolai_vatutin
                    is_character = SOV_Ivan_konev
                    is_character = SOV_Semyon_timoshenko
                    is_character = SOV_Kliment_voroshilov_military
                    is_character = SOV_Kliment_voroshilov_advisor
                    is_character = SOV_Mikhail_tukhachevsky
                    is_character = SOV_Semyon_budyonny
                    is_character = SOV_Ivan_chernyakhovsky
                    is_character = SOV_Issa_pliyev
                    is_character = SOV_Leonid_govorov

                    is_character = SOV_Andrey_yeryomenko

                    is_character = SOV_Nikolai_berzarin
                    is_character = SOV_Kirill_moskalenko

                }
            }
            set_character_flag = sov_character_switched_to_sou
            set_nationality = SOJ

    }
    SOJ = {
        create_faction = sov_comintern_faction
        if = {
            limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
            load_oob = "SOJ_civil_war_BBA"
        }
        else = {
            load_oob = "SOJ_civil_war_legacy"
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = {
                    has_dlc = "No Step Back"
                }

            load_oob = "SOJ_civil_war"
        }
        else_if = {

    }
}

#Setup CRI
sov_spawn_cri_scw = {
    CRI = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                137 = {
                    NOT = {
                        is_core_of = CRI
                    }
                }
            }
            add_state_core = 137
        }
        transfer_state = 137
        set_politics = {
            ruling_party = democratic
            elections_allowed = no
        }
        add_ideas = CRI_Neutral_zone
        division_template = {
            name = "Crimean Infantry"
            is_locked = no

            regiments = {
                infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
                infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
                infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
                infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
                infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
                infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
                infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
                infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
                infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
            }
            support = {
                artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
            }
        }
        random_owned_controlled_state = {
            create_unit = {
                division = "name = \"1st Crimean Infantry\" division_template = \"Crimean Infantry\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
                owner = CRI
            }
            create_unit = {
                division = "name = \"2nd Crimean Infantry\" division_template = \"Crimean Infantry\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
                owner = CRI
            }
            create_unit = {
                division = "name = \"3rd Crimean Infantry\" division_template = \"Crimean Infantry\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
                owner = CRI
            }
            create_unit = {
                division = "name = \"4th Crimean Infantry\" division_template = \"Crimean Infantry\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
                owner = CRI
            }
        }
    }
}

#Setup UKR
sov_spawn_ukr_scw = {
    every_state = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                is_owned_by = SOV
                is_owned_by = SOJ
            }
            is_core_of = UKR
        }
        UKR = {
            transfer_state = PREV
        }
    }
    UKR = {
        add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
            type = motorized_equipment_1
            amount = 200
            producer = UKR
        }
        add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
            type = fighter_equipment_0
            amount = 100
            producer = UKR
        }
        add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
            type = infantry_equipment_0
            amount = 1000
            producer = UKR
        }
        add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
            type = support_equipment_1
            amount = 100
            producer = UKR
        }
        add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
            type = artillery_equipment_1
            amount = 100
            producer = UKR
        }
        division_template = {
            name = "Patrul'nyy Triad Militsiyi"
            is_locked = no
            division_names_group = UKR_CAV_01

            regiments = {
                cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
                cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
                cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
                cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
            }
            support = 	{
                military_police = { x = 0 y = 0 }
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                is_subject = yes
            }
            OVERLORD = {
                set_autonomy = {
                    target = UKR
                    autonomy_state = autonomy_free
                }
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                is_in_faction = yes
            }
            leave_faction = yes
        }
        set_politics = {
            ruling_party = neutrality
        }
        add_ideas = UKR_Provisional_government
        set_country_flag = ukr_anarchist_rebels
        country_event = { id = russia2_ukraine.91 days = 5 }
        #Balancing
        random_owned_state = {
            add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
            add_building_construction = {
                type = arms_factory
                level = 3
                instant_build = yes
            }
        }
        country_lock_all_division_template = no
        division_template = {
            name = "Ukrayins'ka Dyviziya"
            division_names_group = UKR_INF_01
            priority = 1
            regiments = {
                infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
                infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
                infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
                infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
                infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
                infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
                infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
                infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
                infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
            }
            support = {
                engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
                artillery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
            }
        }
        division_template = {
            name = "Ukrayins'ka mekhanizovana Dyviziya"
            division_names_group = UKR_UKR_01
            priority = 1
            regiments = {
                light_armor = { x = 0 y = 0 }
                light_armor = { x = 0 y = 1 }
                light_armor = { x = 1 y = 0 }
                light_armor = { x = 1 y = 1 }
                light_armor = { x = 1 y = 2 }
                motorized = { x = 2 y = 0 }
                motorized = { x = 2 y = 1 }
                motorized = { x = 2 y = 2 }
                motorized = { x = 2 y = 3 }
            }
            support = {
                engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
            }
        }
        201 = {
            create_unit = {
                division = "name = \"1ya Ukrayins'ka Dyviziya\" division_template = \"Ukrayins'ka Dyviziya\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
                owner = UKR
                prioritize_location = 9493
            }
            create_unit = {
                division = "name = \"2ya Ukrayins'ka Dyviziya\" division_template = \"Ukrayins'ka Dyviziya\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
                owner = UKR
                prioritize_location = 11477
            }
            create_unit = {
                division = "name = \"3ya Ukrayins'ka Dyviziya\" division_template = \"Ukrayins'ka Dyviziya\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
                owner = UKR
                prioritize_location = 9466
            }
        }

#Rebalance Industry - Civil War
sov_rebalance_industry_scw = {
    set_temp_variable = { balance_civs_count = 0 }
    while_loop_effect = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                var = balance_civs_count
                value = 8
                compare = less_than
            }
        }
        random_owned_state = {
            limit = {
                NOT = {
                    state = 194
                    state = 204
                    state = 241
                    state = 206
                    state = 207
                    state = 201
                    state = 199
                    state = 198
                    state = 192
                    state = 197
                    state = 196
                    state = 200
                    state = 227
                    state = 228
                    state = 221
                    state = 226
                    state = 203
                    state = 259
                    state = 225
                    state = 193
                    state = 202
                    state = 137
                    state = 231
                    state = 230
                    state = 229
                    state = 590
                    state = 583
                    state = 402
                    state = 587
                    state = 404
                    state = 586
                    state = 589
                    state = 732
                    state = 742
                    state = 405
                    state = 585
                    state = 584
                }
                industrial_complex > 0
                original_white_province_second_civil_war = no
            }
            remove_building = {
                type = industrial_complex
                level = 1
            }
        }
        random_owned_state = {
            limit = {
                original_white_province_second_civil_war = yes
            }
            add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
            add_building_construction = {
                type = industrial_complex
                level = 1
                instant_build = yes
            }
        }
        add_to_temp_variable = { balance_civs_count = 1 }
    }
    set_temp_variable = { balance_mils_count = 0 }
    while_loop_effect = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                var = balance_mils_count
                value = 5
                compare = less_than
            }
        }
        random_owned_state = {
            limit = {
                NOT = {
                    state = 194
                    state = 204
                    state = 241
                    state = 206
                    state = 207
                    state = 201
                    state = 199
                    state = 198
                    state = 192
                    state = 197
                    state = 196
                    state = 200
                    state = 227
                    state = 228
                    state = 221
                    state = 226
                    state = 203
                    state = 259
                    state = 225
                    state = 193
                    state = 202
                    state = 137
                    state = 231
                    state = 230
                    state = 229
                    state = 590
                    state = 583
                    state = 402
                    state = 587
                    state = 404
                    state = 586
                    state = 589
                    state = 732
                    state = 742
                    state = 405
                    state = 585
                    state = 584
                }
                arms_factory > 0
                original_white_province_second_civil_war = no
            }
            remove_building = {
                type = arms_factory
                level = 1
            }
        }
        random_owned_state = {
            limit = {
                original_white_province_second_civil_war = yes
            }
            add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
            add_building_construction = {
                type = arms_factory
                level = 1
                instant_build = yes
            }
        }
        add_to_temp_variable = { balance_mils_count = 1 }
    }
}

#Spawn Elite Panzer if the Player Bought them
sov_spawn_panzer_scw = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_purchased_panzers_for_civil_war
            }
        }
        SOV = {
            load_oob = "SOV_panzer_elite_civil_war"
        }
    }
}

#Spawn Japanese Elite if the Player Recruited them

    if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_recruited_japanese_elite_for_civil_war
            }
        }
        SOV = {
            load_oob = "SOV_japanese_volunteers_elite_civil_war"
        }
    }
}

#Spawn Japanese Ships if the Player Bought them
sov_spawn_japanese_ships_scw = { #TODO Check OOB
    if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_recruited_japanese_elite_for_civil_war
            }
            has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
        }
        SOV = {
            load_oob = "SOV_japanese_ships_civil_war"
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_recruited_japanese_elite_for_civil_war
            }
            NOT ={
                has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
            }
        }
        SOV = {
            load_oob = "SOV_japanese_ships_civil_war_legacy"
        }
    }
}

#Spawn Italian Volunteers and Mountaineers at the start of the civil war
sov_spawn_italian_volunteers_scw = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_trained_mountaineers_for_civil_war
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = control_caucasus
                }
            }
        }
        SOV = {
            load_oob = "SOV_elite_mountaineers_no_caucasus_civil_war"
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_trained_mountaineers_for_civil_war
                has_country_flag = control_caucasus
            }
        }
        SOV = {
            load_oob = "SOV_elite_mountaineers_has_caucasus_civil_war"
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_engaged_italian_division_for_civil_war
            }
        }
        SOV = {
            load_oob = "SOV_italian_volunteers_caucasus_civil_war"
        }
    }
}

#Event to Spawn English Ships and Marines at the start of the civil war
sov_spawn_english_ships_marines_scw = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_bought_english_ships_for_civil_war
                has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
            }
        }
        SOV = {
            load_oob = "SOV_english_naval_ships_civil_war"
        }
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_bought_english_ships_for_civil_war
                NOT = {
                    has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
                }
            }
        }
        SOV = {
            load_oob = "SOV_english_naval_ships_legacy_civil_war"
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            SOV = {
                has_country_flag = has_trained_russian_marine_for_civil_war
            }
        }
        SOV = {
            set_technology = {
                marines = 1
            }
            load_oob = "SOV_elite_marines_civil_war"
        }
    }
}

sov_clean_scw_arrays = {
    for_each_loop = {
        array = global.russian_scw_participants

        if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    OR = {
                        tag = D01
                        tag = D02
                        tag = D03
                        tag = D04
                        tag = D05
                        tag = D06
                        tag = D07
                        tag = D08
                        tag = D09
                        tag = D10
                        tag = D11
                        tag = D12
                        tag = D13
                        tag = D14
                        tag = D15
                        tag = D16
                        tag = D17
                        tag = D18
                        tag = D19
                        tag = D20
                        tag = D21
                        tag = D22
                        tag = D23
                        tag = D24
                        tag = D25
                        tag = D26
                        tag = D27
                        tag = D28
                        tag = D29
                        tag = D30
                        tag = D31
                        tag = D32
                        tag = D33
                        tag = D34
                        tag = D35
                        tag = D36
                        tag = D37
                        tag = D38
                        tag = D39
                        tag = D40
                        tag = D41
                        tag = D42
                        tag = D43
                        tag = D44
                        tag = D45
                        tag = D46
                        tag = D47
                        tag = D48
                        tag = D49
                        tag = D50
                    }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        OR = {
                            NOT = {
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        sov_in_scw = yes
                                    }
                                    has_war_with = SOV
                                }
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        soj_in_scw = yes
                                    }
                                    has_war_with = SOJ
                                }
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        ukr_in_scw = yes
                                    }
                                    has_war_with = UKR
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants = var:v }
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = var:v }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = var:v }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = var:v }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = var:v }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = var:v }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = var:v }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_other = var:v }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_other = var:v }
            }
        }
    }

    for_each_scope_loop = {
        array = global.russian_scw_participants

        if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    exists = no
                    NOT = {
                        has_global_flag = second_russian_civil_war_in_progress
                    }
                    NOT = {
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                sov_in_scw = yes
                            }
                            has_war_with = SOV
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                soj_in_scw = yes
                            }
                            has_war_with = SOJ
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                ukr_in_scw = yes
                            }
                            has_war_with = UKR
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants = THIS }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants = THIS }
                log = " Removed [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) from global.russian_scw_participants array"
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = THIS }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = THIS }
                log = " Removed [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) from global.russian_scw_participants_sov array"
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = THIS }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = THIS }
                log = " Removed [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) from global.russian_scw_participants_soj array"
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = THIS }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = THIS }
                log = " Removed [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) from global.russian_scw_participants_ukr array"
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_other = THIS }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_other = THIS }
                log = " Removed [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) from global.russian_scw_participants_other array"
            }
        }
        else = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = THIS }
                    OR = {
                        NOT = {
                            tag = SOV
                            is_in_faction_with = SOV
                            is_subject_of = SOV
                        }
                        sov_in_scw = no
                    }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = THIS }
                log = " Removed [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) from global.russian_scw_participants_sov array"
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = THIS }
                    OR = {
                        NOT = {
                            tag = SOJ
                            is_in_faction_with = SOJ
                            is_subject_of = SOJ
                        }
                        soj_in_scw = no
                    }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = THIS }
                log = " Removed [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) from global.russian_scw_participants_soj array"
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = THIS }
                    OR = {
                        NOT = {
                            tag = UKR
                            is_in_faction_with = UKR
                            is_subject_of = UKR
                        }
                        ukr_in_scw = no
                    }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = THIS }
                log = " Removed [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) from global.russian_scw_participants_ukr array"
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_other = THIS }
                    OR = {
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = THIS }
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = THIS }
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = THIS }
                        AND = {
                            NOT = {
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        sov_in_scw = yes
                                    }
                                    has_war_with = SOV
                                }
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        sov_in_scw = yes
                                    }
                                    has_war_with = SOJ
                                }
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        ukr_in_scw = yes
                                    }
                                    has_war_with = UKR
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                remove_from_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_other = THIS }
                log = " Removed [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) from global.russian_scw_participants_other array"
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = THIS }
                    }
                    OR = {
                        tag = SOV
                        is_in_faction_with = SOV
                        is_subject_of = SOV
                    }
                    sov_in_scw = yes
                }
                add_to_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = THIS }
                log = " Added [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) to global.russian_scw_participants_sov array"
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = THIS }
                    }
                    OR = {
                        tag = SOJ
                        is_in_faction_with = SOJ
                        is_subject_of = SOJ
                    }
                    soj_in_scw = yes
                }
                add_to_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = THIS }
                log = " Added [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) to global.russian_scw_participants_soj array"
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = THIS }
                    }
                    OR = {
                        tag = UKR
                        is_in_faction_with = UKR
                        is_subject_of = UKR
                    }
                    ukr_in_scw = yes
                }
                add_to_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = THIS }
                log = " Added [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) to global.russian_scw_participants_ukr array"
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = {
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_other = THIS }
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_sov = THIS }
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_soj = THIS }
                        is_in_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_ukr = THIS }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                sov_in_scw = yes
                            }
                            tag = SOV
                            is_in_faction_with = SOV
                            is_subject_of = SOV
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                soj_in_scw = yes
                            }
                            tag = SOJ
                            is_in_faction_with = SOJ
                            is_subject_of = SOJ
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                ukr_in_scw = yes
                            }
                            tag = UKR
                            is_in_faction_with = UKR
                            is_subject_of = UKR
                        }
                    }
                    OR = {
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                sov_in_scw = yes
                            }
                            has_war_with = SOV
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                sov_in_scw = yes
                            }
                            has_war_with = SOJ
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                ukr_in_scw = yes
                            }
                            has_war_with = UKR
                        }
                    }
                }
                add_to_array = { global.russian_scw_participants_other = THIS }
                log = " Added [THIS.GetNameDefCap] ([THIS.GetTag]) to global.russian_scw_participants_other array"
            }
        }
    }
}
#End of Second Civil War

#Increase Great Purge Penalties
sov_increase_great_purge_penalties = {
    custom_effect_tooltip = sov_will_increase_purge_penalties_tt
    subtract_from_variable = { army_org_factor_great_purge = 0.02 }
    clamp_variable = {
        var = army_org_factor_great_purge
        min = var:army_org_factor_great_purge_max
        max = 0
    }
    subtract_from_variable = { send_volunteer_factor_great_purge = 0.02 }
    clamp_variable = {
        var = send_volunteer_factor_great_purge
        min = var:send_volunteer_factor_great_purge_max
        max = 0
    }
    subtract_from_variable = { army_attack_factor_great_purge = 0.02 }
    clamp_variable = {
        var = army_attack_factor_great_purge
        min = var:army_attack_factor_great_purge_max
        max = 0
    }
    subtract_from_variable = { army_defence_factor_great_purge = 0.02 }
    clamp_variable = {
        var = army_defence_factor_great_purge
        min = var:army_defence_factor_great_purge_max
        max = 0
    }
    subtract_from_variable = { party_popularity_stability_factor_great_purge = 0.02 }
    clamp_variable = {
        var = party_popularity_stability_factor_great_purge
        min = var:party_popularity_stability_factor_great_purge_max
        max = 0
    }
    subtract_from_variable = { experience_gain_army_factor_great_purge = 0.02 }
    clamp_variable = {
        var = experience_gain_army_factor_great_purge
        min = var:experience_gain_army_factor_great_purge_max
        max = 0
    }
    add_to_variable = { training_time_factor_great_purge = 0.02 }
    clamp_variable = {
        var = training_time_factor_great_purge
        min = 0
        max = var:training_time_factor_great_purge_max
    }
    add_to_variable = { political_advisor_cost_factor_great_purge = 0.02 }
    clamp_variable = {
        var = political_advisor_cost_factor_great_purge
        min = 0
        max = var:political_advisor_cost_factor_great_purge_max
    }
    hidden_effect = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    var = sov_great_purge_completion
                    value = 100
                    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
            }
            country_event = russia2_russia.25
            clr_country_flag = sov_purge_ongoing
        }
    }
}

#Calculate Democratic Custom GUI Bar Progress
calculate_sov_gui_percentage_democratic_vote = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = {
                    var = current_democratic_vote^0
                    value = 1
                    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
                check_variable = {
                    var = current_democratic_vote^1
                    value = 1
                    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
            }
        }
        set_variable = { sov_gui_percentage_democratic_vote = current_democratic_vote^0 }
        divide_variable = { sov_gui_percentage_democratic_vote = current_democratic_vote_registered^num }
        multiply_variable = { sov_gui_percentage_democratic_vote = 100 }
        round_variable = sov_gui_percentage_democratic_vote
        clamp_variable = {
            var = sov_gui_percentage_democratic_vote
            min = 0
            max = 100
        }
    }
    else = {
        set_variable = { sov_gui_percentage_democratic_vote = 50 }
    }
}

ukr_check_continents_triggers = {
    set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@europe = 0 }
    set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@north_america = 0 }
    set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@south_america = 0 }
    set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@australia = 0 }
    set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@africa = 0 }
    set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@asia = 0 }
    set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@middle_east = 0 }

    for_each_loop = {
        array = ukr.anarchist_states
        value = v
        index = i
        break = break_array

        if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    is_on_continent = europe
                    is_core_of = UKR
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@europe = 0 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    is_on_continent = north_america
                    is_core_of = UKR
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@north_america = 0 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    is_on_continent = south_america
                    is_core_of = UKR
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@south_america = 0 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    is_on_continent = australia
                    is_core_of = UKR
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@australia = 0 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    is_on_continent = africa
                    is_core_of = UKR
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@africa = 0 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    is_on_continent = asia
                    is_core_of = UKR
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@asia = 0 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    is_on_continent = middle_east
                    is_core_of = UKR
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_continent_cores@middle_east = 0 }
        }
    }
}

#Update the state list
ukr_update_anarchist_states = {
    #First, update the main array ukr.controlled_states
    resize_array = { ukr.anarchist_states = 0 }
    for_each_loop = {
        array = ukr.controlled_states
        value = v
        index = i
        break = break_array

        add_to_array = { ukr.anarchist_states = var:v }
    }

    #Update the daily gain of states
    ukr_check_continents_triggers = yes

    for_each_loop = {
        array = ukr.anarchist_states
        value = v
        index = i
        break = break_array

        if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    is_controlled_by = UKR
                }
            }
            #Base gain is 0.4
            set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.4 }

            #Continent popularity
            if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_on_continent = europe
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_malus_europe_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    subtract_from_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_bonus_europe_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_on_continent = north_america
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_malus_north_america_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    subtract_from_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_bonus_north_america_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_on_continent = south_america
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_malus_south_america_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    subtract_from_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_bonus_south_america_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_on_continent = australia
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_malus_australia_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    subtract_from_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_bonus_australia_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_on_continent = africa
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_malus_africa_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    subtract_from_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_bonus_africa_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_on_continent = asia
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_malus_asia_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    subtract_from_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_bonus_asia_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_on_continent = middle_east
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_malus_middle_east_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    subtract_from_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        ukr_bonus_middle_east_anarchist_states = yes
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.2 }
                }
            }

            #Core
            if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_core_of = UKR
                    }
                }
                add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.8 }
            }

            #Boost
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = {
                        var = ukr.anarchist_support_boost@var:v
                        value = 0
                        compare = greater_than
                    }
                }
                add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v = 0.5 }
            }

            clamp_variable = {
                var = ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v
                min = 0
                max = 2
            }
        }
    }
}

#Add daily gain
ukr_add_daily_gain_anarchist_states = {
    for_each_loop = {
        array = ukr.anarchist_states
        value = v
        index = i
        break = break_array

        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    var = ukr.anarchist_support@var:v
                    value = 100
                    compare = less_than
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support@var:v = ukr.anarchist_support_daily@var:v }
            clamp_variable = {
                var = ukr.anarchist_support@var:v
                min = 0
                max = 100
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                var:v = {
                    is_core_of = UKR
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        has_dynamic_modifier = {
                            modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_non_converted
                        }
                    }
                }
                var:v = {
                    remove_dynamic_modifier = {
                        modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_non_converted
                    }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        has_dynamic_modifier = {
                            modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_converted
                        }
                    }
                }
                var:v = {
                    remove_dynamic_modifier = {
                        modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_converted
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        else = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = {
                        var = ukr.anarchist_support@var:v
                        value = 100
                        compare = equals
                    }
                    var:v = {
                        NOT = {
                            has_dynamic_modifier = {
                                modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_converted
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                var:v = {
                    add_dynamic_modifier = {
                        modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_converted
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        var:v = {
                            has_dynamic_modifier = {
                                modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_non_converted
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    var:v = {
                        remove_dynamic_modifier = {
                            modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_non_converted
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = {
                        var = ukr.anarchist_support@var:v
                        value = 100
                        compare = less_than
                    }
                    var:v = {
                        NOT = {
                            has_dynamic_modifier = {
                                modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_non_converted
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                var:v = {
                    add_dynamic_modifier = {
                        modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_non_converted
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        var:v = {
                            has_dynamic_modifier = {
                                modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_converted
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    var:v = {
                        remove_dynamic_modifier = {
                            modifier = ukr_anarchist_state_converted
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = {
                    check_variable = {
                        var = ukr.anarchist_support_boost@var:v
                        value = 0
                        compare = equals
                    }
                }
            }
            subtract_from_variable = { ukr.anarchist_support_boost@var:v = 1 }
            clamp_variable = {
                var = ukr.anarchist_support_boost@var:v
                min = 0
                max = 30
            }
        }
    }

    set_temp_variable = { ukr_daily_anarchy_gain_temp = 0 }

    for_each_loop = {
        array = ukr.anarchist_states
        value = v
        index = i
        break = break_array


        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    var = ukr.anarchist_support@var:v
                    value = 100
                    compare = equals
                }
                var:v = {
                    is_core_of = UKR
                }
            }
            add_to_temp_variable = { ukr_daily_anarchy_gain_temp = 0.05 }
        }
    }

    set_variable = { ukr_anarchist_daily_gain = var:ukr_daily_anarchy_gain_temp }
    force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
}

#Update the state cost
ukr_update_state_cost = {
    for_each_loop = {
        array = ukr.anarchist_states
        value = v
        index = i
        break = break_array

        var:v = {
            set_temp_variable = { state_boost_cost = THIS.state_and_terrain_strategic_value }
            multiply_temp_variable = { state_boost_cost = 5 }
            round_temp_variable = state_boost_cost
            clamp_temp_variable = {
                var = state_boost_cost
                min = 25
                max = 250
            }
            set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_state_boost_cost@THIS = var:state_boost_cost }

            set_temp_variable = { state_core_cost = THIS.state_population_k }
            divide_temp_variable = { state_core_cost = 10 }
            set_temp_variable = { state_core_cost_multiplier = ukr.anarchist_support@THIS }
            divide_temp_variable = { state_core_cost_multiplier = 100 }
            divide_temp_variable = { state_core_cost = state_core_cost_multiplier }
            clamp_temp_variable = {
                var = state_core_cost
                min = 10
                max = 500
            }
            set_variable = { ukr.anarchist_state_core_cost@THIS = var:state_core_cost }
        }
    }
}

#Update current view
ukr_update_current_view = {
    resize_array = { ukr.anarchist_states_current_view = 0 }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                var = ukr.view_anarchist_states_can_be_cored
                value = 2
                compare = equals
            }
        }
        for_each_loop = {
            array = ukr.anarchist_states
            value = v
            index = i
            break = break_array

            if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_controlled_by = UKR
                        NOT = {
                            is_core_of = UKR
                        }
                        check_variable = {
                            var = ukr.political_power
                            value = ukr.anarchist_state_core_cost@var:v
                            compare = greater_than_or_equals
                        }
                        any_neighbor_state = {
                            is_core_of = UKR
                        }
                        check_variable = {
                            var = ukr.anarchist_support@var:v
                            value = 50
                            compare = greater_than_or_equals
                        }
                        check_variable = {
                            var = ukr.anarchist_coring_points
                            value = 1
                            compare = greater_than_or_equals
                        }
                    }
                }
                add_to_array = { ukr.anarchist_states_current_view = var:v }
            }
        }
    }
    else = {
        for_each_loop = {
            array = ukr.anarchist_states
            value = v
            index = i
            break = break_array

            if = {
                limit = {
                    var:v = {
                        is_controlled_by = UKR
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                NOT = {
                                    check_variable = {
                                        var = ukr.view_anarchist_states_core
                                        value = 2
                                        compare = equals
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            NOT = {
                                is_core_of = UKR
                            }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                NOT = {
                                    check_variable = {
                                        var = ukr.view_anarchist_states_converted
                                        value = 2
                                        compare = equals
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            check_variable = {
                                var = ukr.anarchist_support@var:v
                                value = 100
                                compare = less_than
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                add_to_array = { ukr.anarchist_states_current_view = var:v }
            }
        }
    }
}

ukr_spawn_free_division_decision_scripted_effect = {
    random_owned_controlled_state = {
        limit = {
            is_core_of = FROM
            NOT = {
                is_capital = yes
            }
        }
        create_unit = {
            division = "name = \"Zvil'nennya Dyviziya\" division_template = \"Zvil'nennya Dyviziya\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
            owner = ROOT
            allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
        }
        create_unit = {
            division = "name = \"Zvil'nennya Dyviziya\" division_template = \"Zvil'nennya Dyviziya\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
            owner = ROOT

set_variable_for_winning_anarchist_party_election = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                var = sov_anarchist_election_current_ruling_party
                value = 0
                compare = equals
            }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = research_anarchist_election_bonus_3_months
        hidden_effect = {
            set_variable = { anarchy_intellect_party_research = 0.10 }
        }
        random_tech_anarchist_election = yes
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                var = sov_anarchist_election_current_ruling_party
                value = 1
                compare = equals
            }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = civilian_industry_anarchist_election_bonus_3_months
        set_variable = { anarchy_industry_party_factory = 0.10 }
        set_variable = { anarchy_industry_party_resources = 0.25 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                var = sov_anarchist_election_current_ruling_party
                value = 2
                compare = equals
            }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = military_industry_anarchist_election_bonus_3_months
        set_variable = { anarchy_military_industry_party_guns = 0.15 }
        set_variable = { anarchy_military_industry_party_guns_fabrication = 0.1 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                var = sov_anarchist_election_current_ruling_party
                value = 3
                compare = equals
            }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = militarist_bonus_anarchist_election_bonus_3_months
        set_variable = { anarchy_militarist_party_training = -0.15 }
        set_variable = { anarchy_militarist_party_attack = 0.05 }
        set_variable = { anarchy_militarist_party_defence = 0.05 }
        set_variable = { anarchy_militarist_party_organization = 0.05 }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_variable = {
                var = sov_anarchist_election_current_ruling_party

                compare = equals
            }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = aviation_bonus_anarchist_election_bonus_3_months

        set_variable = { anarchy_aviation_party_ace_generation = 0.25 }
        set_variable = { anarchy_aviation_party_attack = 0.05 }

        set_variable = { anarchy_aviation_party_agility = 0.05 }

        set_variable = { anarchy_ship_party_dockyard_speed = 0.1 }
        hidden_effect = {
            random_list = {
                25 = {

                        load_oob = "SOV_destroyer_anarchist"

                    }
                }
                10 = {

                    }
                }
            }

    }
    if = {
        limit = {

                compare = equals

        custom_effect_tooltip = logistic_bonus_anarchist_election_bonus_3_months

# damn thats some great coding there Paradox
sov_unlock_nkvd_chiefs = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_character = SOV_Genrikh_yagoda
        }
        if = { #If active, keep him active after changing his role
            limit = {
                has_idea = SOV_Genrikh_yagoda
            }
            remove_advisor_role = {
                character = SOV_Genrikh_yagoda
                slot = political_advisor
            }
            add_advisor_role = {
                character = SOV_Genrikh_yagoda
                advisor = {
                    slot = political_advisor
                    idea_token = SOV_Genrikh_yagoda
                    cost = 50

                    allowed = {
                        original_tag = SOV
                    }

                    available = {
                        has_government = communism
                        NOT = {
                            has_idea = SOV_Nikolay_yezhov
                            has_idea = SOV_Lavrentiy_beria

                                tooltip = SOV_idea_not_purged_tt

                                        var = sov_great_purge_status^1
                                        value = 2
                                        compare = equals
                                    }
                                    has_character_flag = SOV_purge_politician_trotsky_russia
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    traits = {
                        russia2_state_security_administrator_2
                        russia2_head_nkvd
                    }

                        factor = 5
                    }
                }
                activate = yes
            }
        }

            remove_advisor_role = {

                slot = political_advisor

#Just in Case
SOV_unlock_propaganda_campaign_slot_effect_russia2 = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_left_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_locked_slot_index }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_left_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SOV_poster_center_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_locked_slot_index }
			}
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_center_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { SOV_poster_right_icon_frame = SOV_propaganda_empty_slot_index }
		}
	}
}

sov_transfer_baltic_puppet_scw = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            LIT = {
                is_subject_of = SOV
                has_civil_war = yes
                has_government = communism
            }
        }
        every_country = {
            limit = {
                original_tag = LIT
                NOT = {
                    has_government = communism
                }
            }
            LIT = {
                annex_country = {
                    target = PREV
                }
            }
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            LAT = {
                is_subject_of = SOV
                has_civil_war = yes
                has_government = communism
            }
        }
        every_country = {
            limit = {
                original_tag = LAT
                NOT = {
                    has_government = communism
                }
            }
            LAT = {
                annex_country = {
                    target = PREV
                }
            }
        }
    }
    if = {
        limit = {
            EST = {
                is_subject_of = SOV
                has_civil_war = yes
                has_government = communism
            }
        }
        every_country = {
            limit = {
                original_tag = EST
                NOT = {
                    has_government = communism
                }
            }
            EST = {
                annex_country = {
                    target = PREV
                }
            }
        }
    }
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            is_subject_of = SOV
            has_government = communism
        }
        SOJ = {
            set_autonomy = {
                target = PREV
                autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
            }
        }
    }
}
